\x53\x75\x61\x73\x61\x6e\x61\x20\x64\x61\x6c\x61\x6d\x20\x62\x69\x6c\x69\x6b\x20\x62\x61\x63\x61\x61\x6e\x20\x69\x74\x75\x20\x73\x75\x72\x61\x6d\x2c\x20\x64\x69\x74\x61\x6d\x62\x61\x68\x20\x64\x65\x6e\x67\x61\x6e\x20\x77\x61\x6a\x61\x68\x20\x77\x61\x6a\x61\x68\x20\x6d\x75\x72\x61\x6d\x20\x73\x69\x20\x69\x62\x75\x20\x64\x61\x6e\x20\x73\x69\x20\x61\x6e\x61\x6b\x20\x79\x61\x6e\x67\x20\x74\x65\x6e\x61\x6e\x67\x20\x6d\x65\x6e\x64\x65\x6e\x67\x61\x72\x20\x62\x69\x63\x61\x72\x61\x20\x70\x65\x67\x75\x61\x6d\x20\x74\x65\x6e\x74\x61\x6e\x67\x20\x77\x61\x73\x69\x61\x74\x20\x73\x69\x20\x61\x79\x61\x68\x20\x79\x61\x6e\x67\x20\x62\x61\x72\x75\x20\x73\x61\x68\x61\x6a\x61\x20\x6d\x65\x6e\x69\x6e\x67\x67\x61\x6c\x20\x64\x75\x6e\x69\x61\x20\x61\x6b\x69\x62\x61\x74\x20\x70\x65\x6e\x79\x61\x6b\x69\x74\x20\x6b\x61\x6e\x73\x65\x72\x2e\x20\x50\x65\x67\x75\x61\x6d\x20\x69\x74\x75\x20\x6d\x65\x6e\x67\x65\x6c\x75\x61\x72\x6b\x61\x6e\x20\x73\x61\x6d\x70\x75\x6c\x20\x62\x65\x73\x61\x72\x20\x62\x65\x72\x73\x61\x69\x7a\x20\x41\x34\x20\x64\x61\x72\x69\x70\x61\x64\x61\x20\x62\x65\x67\x20\x68\x69\x74\x61\x6d\x6e\x79\x61\x20\x79\x61\x6e\x67\x20\x62\x65\x72\x69\x73\x69\x20\x73\x65\x62\x61\x74\x61\x6e\x67\x20\x6c\x6f\x6c\x69\x70\x6f\x70\x20\x62\x65\x72\x77\x61\x72\x6e\x61\x20\x77\x61\x72\x6e\x69\x20\x64\x61\x6e\x20\x73\x65\x6b\x65\x70\x69\x6e\x67\x20\x73\x75\x72\x61\x74\x20\x64\x69\x6c\x69\x70\x61\x74\x20\x6b\x65\x6d\x61\x73\x2e\x20\x4b\x61\x74\x61\x20\x70\x65\x67\x75\x61\x6d\x2c\x20\x70\x65\x6e\x69\x6e\x67\x67\x61\x6c\x61\x6e\x20\x73\x69\x20\x61\x79\x61\x68\x20\x75\x6e\x74\x75\x6b\x20\x73\x69\x20\x69\x62\x75\x20\x63\x75\x6d\x61\x20\x6c\x61\x68\x20\x73\x65\x62\x61\x74\x61\x6e\x67\x20\x6c\x6f\x6c\x69\x70\x6f\x70\x20\x62\x65\x72\x77\x61\x72\x6e\x61\x20\x77\x61\x72\x6e\x69\x2c\x20\x6d\x61\x6e\x61\x6b\x61\x6c\x61\x20\x73\x69\x20\x61\x6e\x61\x6b\x20\x74\x69\x64\x61\x6b\x20\x61\x6b\x61\x6e\x20\x6d\x65\x77\x61\x72\x69\x73\x69\x20\x61\x70\x61\x20\x61\x70\x61\x20\x70\x75\x6e\x20\x6d\x65\x6c\x61\x69\x6e\x6b\x61 \x61\x74\x20\x73\x75\x6e\x61\x74\x20\x44\x68\x75\x68\x61\x2e\x0a\x0a\x20\xe2\x80\x9c\x53\x61\x66\x69\x2c\x20\x6d\x61\x72\x69\x20\x6b\x65\x6c\x75\x61\x72\x20\x63\x65\x70\x61\x74\x2e\xe2\x80\x9d\x20\x70\x69\x6e\x74\x61\x20\x69\x62\x75\x6e\x79\x61\x20\x64\x61\x72\x69\x20\x72\x75\x61\x6e\x67\x20\x74\x61\x6d\x75\x2e\x20\x20\x41\x79\x61\x68\x6e\x79\x61\x20\x62\x65\x72\x61\x64\x61\x20\x64\x69\x20\x6b\x65\x62\x75\x6e\x2e\x0a\x0a\xe2\x80\x9c\x53\x65\x62\x65\x6e\x74\x61\x72\x2c\x20\x65\x6d\x61\x6b\x2e\x20\x4c\x69\x6d\x61\x20\x6d\x69\x6e\x69\x74\x20\x6c\x61\x67\x69\x20\x53\x61\x66\x69\x20\x64\x61\x74\x61\x6e\x67\xe2\x80\x9d\x20\x73\x61\x68\x75\x74\x20\x53\x61\x66\x69\x20\x79\x61\x6e\x67\x20\x6d\x61\x73\x69\x68\x20\x62\x65\x72\x74\x65\x6c\x65\x6b\x75\x6e\x67\x2e\x20\x49\x6e\x69\x20\x72\x6f\x6d\x62\x6f\x6e\x67\x61\x6e\x20\x6d\x65\x6d\x69\x6e\x61\x6e\x67\x20\x6b\x61\x6c\x69\x20\x6b\x65\x64\x75\x61\x2e\x20\x50\x69\x6e\x61\x6e\x67\x61\x6e\x20\x70\x65\x72\x74\x61\x6d\x61\x20\x73\x75\x64\x61\x68\x20\x64\x69\x74\x6f\x6c\x61\x6b\x2e\x20\x41\x79\x61\x68\x6e\x79\x61\x20\x6b\x65\x63\x65\x77\x61\x2e\x20\x4a\x75\x73\x74\x65\x72\x75\x2c\x20\x53\x61\x66\x69\x79\x61\x68\x20\x6d\x65\x6d\x62\x75\x61\x74\x20\x6b\x65\x70\x75\x74\x75\x73\x61\x6e\x20\x75\x6e\x74\x75\x6b\x20\x6d\x65\x6d\x69\x6e\x74\x61\x20\x70\x65\x72\x74\x6f\x6c\x6f\x6e\x67\x61\x6e\x20\x64\x61\x72\x69\x70\x61\x64\x61\x20\x41\x6c\x6c\x61\x68\x20\x64\x65\x6e\x67\x61\x6e\x20\x6d\x65\x6c\x61\x6b\x75\x6b\x61\x6e\x20\x73\x6f\x6c\x61\x74\x20\x69\x73\x74\x69\x6b\x68\x61\x72\x61\x68\x2e\x20\x53\x65\x6c\x65\x73\x61\x69\x20\x73\x61\x68\x61\x6a\x61\x20\x73\x6f\x6c\x61\x74\x2c\x20\x77\x61\x6a\x61\x68\x20\x49\x73\x6b\x61\x6e\x64\x61\x72\x20\x73\x61\x68\x61\x6a\x61\x20\x79\x61\x6e\x67\x20\x6d\x75\x6e\x63\x75\x6c\x2e\x20\x53\x61\x66\x69\x79\x61\x68\x20\x6d\x65\x6d\x62\x65\x72\x61\x6e\x69\x6b\x61\x6e\x20\x64\x69\x72\x69\x20\x75\x6e\x74\x75\x6b\x20\x62\x65\x72\x74\x65\x6d\x75\x20\x64\x65\x6e\x67\x61\x6e\x20\x6b\x65\x6c\x75\x61\x72\x67\x61\x20\x70\x69
